  var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
  xhr.open('POST', '/shop-assets/proxy/errorlog', true);
  xhr.setRequestHeader('Content-Type', 'application/json');
  xhr.send(JSON.stringify(payload));
}
function JSErrorLogger(){
  var self = this;
  self.handler = function(evt) {
    var obj = {
      "time": new Date().getTime(),
      "event": {
        "message": {

          "page-url": window.location.href
        },
        "severity": "info"
      }
    };
    // Do not call on production
    if (window.location.hostname !== 'www.cvs.com') {
      postErrorLog(obj);
    }
    return true;
  };
  self.JSErrorLogger = function() { window.addEventListener('error', self.handler); }();
}

Applying an adhesive product with tension can produce mechanical trauma to the skin. Stretching can also cause adhesion failure.</p> <p>6. The adhesive of Tegaderm dressing is pressure-sensitive. To tailor a dressing for a special application, use sterile scissors to cut the dressing into desired shapes or sizes before removing the printed liner. For best results and ease of application, cut the pieces so that a portion of the frame remains on at least two sides.</p> <p>Removal Hints: Support the skin when removing Tegaderm dressing. For removal from I.V. sites, also stabilize the catheter to prevent dislodgment. Use one of the following removal techniques based on your patient's skin condition and your own personal preference: Gently grasp one edge and slowly peel the dressing from the skin in the direction of hair growth. Try to peel the dressing back over itself, rather than pulling it up from the skin. or Grasp one edge of the dressing and gently pull it straight out to stretch and release adhesion. or Apply an adhesive remover suitable for use on skin to the adhesive edge while gently peeling from the skin. To aid in lifting a dressing edge, secure a piece of surgical tape to one corner and rub firmly. Use the tape as a tab to help you slowly peel back the dressing.</p>","warnings":"Precautions: Stop any bleeding at the site before applying the dressing. Do not stretch the dressing during application as tension can cause skin trauma. Make sure the skin is clean, free of soap residue and lotion and allowed to dry thoroughly before applying the dressing to prevent skin irritation and to ensure good adhesion. The dressing may be used on an infected site, only when under the care of a health care professional. Antimicrobial ointments containing polyethylene glycols may compromise the strength of the Tegaderm HP Transparent Film Dressings. Tegaderm Transparent Dressings should not be re-sterilized by gamma, E-beam or steam methods.               </style></div><div class="css-1dbjc4n r-13qz1uu"><div class="css-1dbjc4n r-13awgt0 r-1mlwlqe" style="max-width:100%"><div class="css-1dbjc4n r-1habvwh r-k200y r-18u37iz r-1wtj0ep r-1sv84sj r-1ur9v65 r-13qz1uu"><h2 aria-level="2" class="css-4rbku5 css-901oao r-1jn44m2 r-zz5t5d r-b88u0q" dir="auto" role="heading">Details</h2><a class="css-4rbku5 css-18t94o4 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1otgn73" data-class="see-all-brand-link" data-focusable="true" href="/shop/brand-shop/t/tegaderm" role="link"><div class="css-901oao r-cme181 r-1jn44m2 r-ubezar r-b88u0q r-vrz42v" dir="auto">See all <!-- -->Tegaderm<!-- --> products &gt;</div></a></div><div class="css-901oao r-1jn44m2 r-1i10wst r-vw2c0b" dir="auto">Tegaderm Transparent Film Dressing 1.75 Length x 1.75 in. Width, 100CT</div><div class="css-901oao r-1jn44m2 r-1enofrn" dir="auto">100 CT, .5 lbs. Item # 546577</div><div class="htmlView" style="max-width:100%"><p>Tegaderm Brand transparent dressings can be used to cover and protect catheter sites and wounds, to maintain a moist environment for wound healing, and to secure devices to the skin.</p><ul><li>Provides a waterproof, sterile barrier to external contaminants including liquids, bacteria and viruses. In vitro testing shows that the transparent film provides a viral barrier from viruses 27 nm in diameter or larger while the dressing remains intact without leakage.</li><li>Made with a hypoallergenic, latex-free adhesive that is gentle to the skin yet holds catheters and other devices in place.</li><li>Conformable: dressing flexes with skin for greater patient comfort.</li><li>Picture-frame delivery makes placement accurate and easy, minimizing potential to stick to gloves or to itself.</li><li>Suggested applications: Short peripheral and midline venous catheters. Clean, closed surgical incisions. Abrasions, skin tears, blisters. Skin graft donor sites. Superficial partial thickness burns. Stage I or II pressure ulcers. Autolytic debridement facilitated by the moist wound healing environment. Protective eye coverings. Post tattoo application and removal.</li><li>Skin care Condition Type: Trauma from Tapes and Dressings.</li><li>Frame style.</li></ul><p><br/>Disclaimer: HCPCS codes have been provided to assist you in the preparation of Medi care Part B claims. Please note, however, that the reimbursement information provided by 3M Health care and its representatives is intended to provide general information relevant to coverage and coding for 3M products. Insurers' reimbursement policies can vary and the use of the codes discussed here does not guarantee that an insurer will cover or pay at any particular level. Health care providers should exercise independent clinical judgment in choosing the codes which most accurately describe the products provided.</p><p> </p><p>This item is FSA (Flexible Spending Account) eligible.</p></div><div class="htmlView" style="max-width:100%"><div id="wc-power-page"></div></div></div><div class="css-1dbjc4n r-13awgt0 r-1mlwlqe" style="max-width:100%"><div class="css-1dbjc4n r-1habvwh r-k200y r-18u37iz r-1wtj0ep r-1sv84sj r-1ur9v65 r-13qz1uu"><div class="css-901oao r-1jn44m2 r-zz5t5d r-b88u0q" dir="auto">Directions</div></div><div class="htmlView" style="max-width:100%"><p>1. Select a dressing size that will adequately cover the catheter and insertion site or wound. Ensure at least a one inch margin of dressing adheres to healthy, dry skin.</p> <p>2. Prepare the catheter insertion site or wound according to your institution's approved protocol.</p> <p>3. To ensure good adhesion, clip excess hair where the dressing will be placed. Do not shave the skin because of the potential for microabrasions.</p> <p>4. Make sure skin is free of soaps, detergents, and lotions. Allow all preps and protectants to dry thoroughly before applying the dressing. Wet preps and soap residues can cause irritation if trapped under the dressing. Additionally, adhesive products do not adhere well to wet or oily surfaces.</p> <p>5. Do not stretch the Tegaderm dressing during application. Applying an adhesive product with tension can produce mechanical trauma to the skin. Stretching can also cause adhesion failure.</p> <p>6. The adhesive of Tegaderm dressing is pressure-sensitive. To ensure best adhesion, always apply firm pressure to the dressing from the center out to the edges.</p> <p>7. To tailor a dressing for a special application, use sterile scissors to cut the dressing into desired shapes or sizes before removing the printed liner. For best results and ease of application, cut the pieces so that a portion of the frame remains on at least two sides.</p> <p>Removal Hints: Support the skin when removing Tegaderm dressing. For removal from I.V. sites, also stabilize the catheter to prevent dislodgment. Use one of the following removal techniques based on your patient's skin condition and your own personal preference: Gently grasp one edge and slowly peel the dressing from the skin in the direction of hair growth. Try to peel the dressing back over itself, rather than pulling it up from the skin. or Grasp one edge of the dressing and gently pull it straight out to stretch and release adhesion. or Apply an adhesive remover suitable for use on skin to the adhesive edge while gently peeling from the skin. To aid in lifting a dressing edge, secure a piece of surgical tape to one corner and rub firmly. Use the tape as a tab to help you slowly peel back the dressing.</p></div></div><div class="css-1dbjc4n r-13awgt0 r-1mlwlqe" style="max-width:100%"><div class="css-1dbjc4n r-1habvwh r-k200y r-18u37iz r-1wtj0ep r-1sv84sj r-1ur9v65 r-13qz1uu"><h2 aria-level="2" class="css-4rbku5 css-901oao r-1jn44m2 r-zz5t5d r-b88u0q" dir="auto" role="heading">Warnings</h2></div><div class="htmlView" style="max-width:100%">Precautions: Stop any bleeding at the site before applying the dressing. Do not stretch the dressing during application as tension can cause skin trauma. Make sure the skin is clean, free of soap residue and lotion and allowed to dry thoroughly before applying the dressing to prevent skin irritation and to ensure good adhesion. The dressing may be used on an infected site, only when under the care of a health care professional. Antimicrobial ointments containing polyethylene glycols may compromise the strength of the Tegaderm HP Transparent Film Dressings. Tegaderm Transparent Dressings should not be re-sterilized by gamma, E-beam or steam methods. Do not use if package is damaged or opened.</div></div><div class="css-1dbjc4n r-9c3h7m r-1mlwlqe r-u04ygo" style="max-width:100%"><div class="css-1dbjc4n r-1habvwh r-k200y r-18u37iz r-1wtj0ep r-1sv84sj r-1ur9v65 r-13qz1uu"><h2 aria-level="2" class="css-4rbku5 css-901oao r-1jn44m2 r-zz5t5d r-b88u0q" dir="auto" role="heading">Reviews</h2></div><div class="css-1dbjc4n r-18u37iz r-95jzfe"><a class="css-4rbku5 css-18t94o4 css-1dbjc4n r-unghlx r-1loqt21 r-1otgn73 r-62p4ah" data-class="write-review-btn" data-focusable="true" href="/shop/review-submission?skuId=546577" role="link"><div class="css-901oao r-jwli3a r-1b43r93 r-vw2c0b r-1cwl3u0 r-1dye5f7 r-23eiwj r-q4m81j" dir="auto">Write a review</div></a></div><div aria-valuemax="1" aria-valuemin="0" class="css-1dbjc4n r-1awozwy r-1777fci" role="progressbar" style="margin-top:80px"><div class="css-1dbjc4n r-17bb2tj r-1muvv40 r-127358a r-1ldzwu0 r-z80fyv r-19wmn03"><svg height="100%" viewbox="0 0 32 32" width="100%"><circle cx="16" cy="16" fill="none" r="14" stroke-width="4" style="stroke:#1976D2;opacity:0.2"></circle><circle cx="16" cy="16" fill="none" r="14" stroke-width="4" style="stroke:#1976D2;stroke-dasharray:80;stroke-dashoffset:60"></circle></svg></div></div></div><div class="css-1dbjc4n r-13awgt0 r-1mlwlqe"><div class="css-1dbjc4n r-1habvwh r-k200y r-18u37iz r-1wtj0ep r-1sv84sj r-1ur9v65 r-13qz1uu"><h2 aria-level="2" class="css-4rbku5 css-901oao r-1jn44m2 r-zz5t5d r-b88u0q" dir="auto" role="heading">Questions &amp;
